			<h1><a  name="&lpos=:editorial" href="/mens-college-basketball/recap?gameId=400988627" class="webview-internal">Creighton beats highest-ranked foe ever in No. 3 Villanova</a></h1>
			
				<p  data-behavior="linkable" data-linkable-href="/mens-college-basketball/recap?gameId=400988627" class="webview-internal" data-linkable-platforms="mobile, tablet">Marcus Foster scored 28 points, Davion Mintz gave Creighton the lead for good early in overtime, and the Bluejays defeated the highest-ranked opponent in program history with an 89-83 upset of No. 3 Villanova on Saturday.</p>
			
		</header>

						function loadScripts() {
							var src = "http://a.espncdn.com/redesign/0.389.10/js/dist/gamepackage-static.min.js",
								script;

							if (espn.gamepackage.status === "in") {
								if (!espn.gamepackage.core) {
									src = src.replace("gamepackage.", "gamepackage.core.");
								} else if (espn.gamepackage.bundles && typeof espn.gamepackage.bundles[espn.gamepackage.sport] === "function") {
									espn.gamepackage.init();
									espn.gamepackage.bundles[espn.gamepackage.sport]();
									return;
								}
							} else if (espn.gamepackage.init) {
								espn.gamepackage.init();
								return;
							}

							script = document.createElement("script");
							script.type = "text/javascript";
							script.src = src;
							document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
						}

						
							if (window.espn_ui.deferReady === true) {
								$(document).one("page.render", loadScripts);
							} else {
								$.subscribe("espn.defer.end", loadScripts);
							}
						

						if( typeof(newrelic) !== "undefined" ){
							newrelic.setCustomAttribute( "game-state", espn.gamepackage.status );
						}
					
				})(jQuery);
